      <p>
       The
       <b>
        Federated States of Micronesia
       </b>
       (
       <span class="nowrap">
        <span class="IPA nopopups noexcerpt">
         <a href="/wiki/Help:IPA/English" title="Help:IPA/English">
          /
          <span style="border-bottom:1px dotted">
           <span title="/ˌ/: secondary stress follows">
            ˌ
           </span>
           <span title="'m' in 'my'">
            m
           </span>
           <span title="/aɪ/: 'i' in 'tide'">
            aɪ
           </span>
           <span title="'k' in 'kind'">
            k
           </span>
           <span title="'r' in 'rye'">
            r
           </span>
           <span title="/oʊ/: 'o' in 'code'">
            oʊ
           </span>
           <span title="/ˈ/: primary stress follows">
            ˈ
           </span>
           <span title="'n' in 'nigh'">
            n
           </span>
           <span title="/iː/: 'ee' in 'fleece'">
            iː
           </span>
           <span title="/ʒ/: 's' in 'pleasure'">
            ʒ
           </span>
           <span title="/ə/: 'a' in 'about'">
            ə
           </span>
          </span>
          /
         </a>
        </span>
        <small class="nowrap">
         (
         <span class="unicode haudio">
          <span class="fn">
           <span style="white-space:nowrap">
            <a href="/wiki/File:En-us-Micronesia.ogg" title="About this sound">
             <img alt="About this sound" data-file-height="20" data-file-width="20" height="11" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/11px-Loudspeaker.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/17px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/8a/Loudspeaker.svg/22px-Loudspeaker.svg.png 2x" width="11"/>
            </a>
           </span>
           <a class="internal" href="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/4/4a/En-us-Micronesia.ogg" title="En-us-Micronesia.ogg">
            listen
           </a>
          </span>
         </span>
         )
        </small>
       </span>
       ; abbreviated
       <b>
        FSM
       </b>
       and also known simply as
       <b>
        Micronesia
       </b>
       ) is an independent
       <a href="/wiki/Sovereign_state" title="Sovereign state">
        sovereign
       </a>
       <a href="/wiki/Island_country" title="Island country">
        island nation
       </a>
       and a
       <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">
        United States
       </a>
       <a href="/wiki/Associated_state" title="Associated state">
        associated state
       </a>
       consisting of four
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Federal_state" title="Federal state">
        states
       </a>
       –  from west to east,
       <a href="/wiki/Yap_State" title="Yap State">
        Yap
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Chuuk_State" title="Chuuk State">
        Chuuk
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Pohnpei_State" title="Pohnpei State">
        Pohnpei
       </a>
       and
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kosrae_State" title="Kosrae State">
        Kosrae
       </a>
       – that are spread across the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Western_Pacific_Ocean" title="Western Pacific Ocean">
        Western Pacific Ocean
       </a>
       . Together, the states comprise around 607 islands (a combined
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Land_area" title="Land area">
        land area
       </a>
       of approximately 702 km
       <sup>
        2
       </sup>
       or 271 sq mi) that cover a
       <a href="/wiki/Longitude" title="Longitude">
        longitudinal
       </a>
       distance of almost 2,700 km (1,678 mi) just north of the
       <a href="/wiki/Equator" title="Equator">
        equator
       </a>
       . They lie northeast of
       <a href="/wiki/New_Guinea" title="New Guinea">
        New Guinea
       </a>
       , south of
       <a href="/wiki/Guam" title="Guam">
        Guam
       </a>
       and the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Marianas" title="Marianas">
        Marianas
       </a>
       , west of
       <a href="/wiki/Nauru" title="Nauru">
        Nauru
       </a>
       and the
       <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Islands" title="Marshall Islands">
        Marshall Islands
       </a>
       , east of
       <a href="/wiki/Palau" title="Palau">
        Palau
       </a>
       and the
       <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">
        Philippines
       </a>
       , about 2,900 km (1,802 mi) north of eastern
       <a href="/wiki/Australia" title="Australia">
        Australia
       </a>
       and some 4,000 km (2,485 mi) southwest of the main islands of
       <a href="/wiki/Hawaii" title="Hawaii">
        Hawaii
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       While the FSM's total land area is quite small, it occupies more than 2,600,000 km
       <sup>
        2
       </sup>
       (1,000,000 sq mi) of the
       <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Ocean" title="Pacific Ocean">
        Pacific Ocean
       </a>
       , giving the country the 14th largest
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Exclusive_Economic_Zone" title="Exclusive Economic Zone">
        Exclusive Economic Zone
       </a>
       in the world.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-4">
        <a href="#cite_note-4">
         [4]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The capital is
       <a href="/wiki/Palikir" title="Palikir">
        Palikir
       </a>
       , located on
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pohnpei_Island" title="Pohnpei Island">
        Pohnpei Island
       </a>
       , while the largest city is
       <a href="/wiki/Weno" title="Weno">
        Weno
       </a>
       , located in the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Chuuk_Atoll" title="Chuuk Atoll">
        Chuuk Atoll
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       Each of its four states is centered on one or more main
       <a href="/wiki/High_island" title="High island">
        high islands
       </a>
       , and all but Kosrae include numerous outlying
       <a href="/wiki/Atoll" title="Atoll">
        atolls
       </a>
       . The Federated States of Micronesia is spread across part of the
       <a href="/wiki/Caroline_Islands" title="Caroline Islands">
        Caroline Islands
       </a>
       in the wider region of
       <a href="/wiki/Micronesia" title="Micronesia">
        Micronesia
       </a>
       , which consists of thousands of small islands divided among several countries. The term
       <i>
        Micronesia
       </i>
       may refer to the Federated States or to the region as a whole.
      </p>
      <p>
       The FSM was formerly a part of the
       <a href="/wiki/Trust_Territory_of_the_Pacific_Islands" title="Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands">
        Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands
       </a>
       (TTPI), a
       <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">
        United Nations
       </a>
       Trust Territory under U.S. administration, but it formed its own constitutional government on May 10, 1979, becoming a sovereign state after independence was attained on November 3, 1986 under a
       <a href="/wiki/Compact_of_Free_Association" title="Compact of Free Association">
        Compact of Free Association
       </a>
       with the United States. Other neighboring island entities, and also former members of the TTPI, formulated their own constitutional governments and became the
       <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Islands" title="Marshall Islands">
        Republic of the Marshall Islands
       </a>
       (RMI) and the
       <a href="/wiki/Palau" title="Palau">
        Republic of Palau
       </a>
       (ROP). The FSM has a seat in the United Nations.
      </p>
      <p>
      </p>

       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/History_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="History of the Federated States of Micronesia">
        History of the Federated States of Micronesia
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="quotebox pullquote" style="float: left; clear: left; margin: 0.5em 1.4em 0.8em 0; width:22em; padding: 10px; border: 1px solid #aaa; font-size: 90%; background-color: #B0C4DE;">
       <div class="" style="background-color: #B0C4DE; color: black; text-align: center; font-size: larger; font-weight: bold;">
        Historical affiliations
       </div>
       <div class="" style="position: relative; text-align: left;">
        <div>
         <span class="flagicon">
          <img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="500" data-file-width="750" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/c/c6/Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg/45px-Flag_of_Spain_%281785-1873_and_1875-1931%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/>
         </span>
         <a href="/wiki/Spain" title="Spain">
          Spain
         </a>
         1887–1899
         <br/>
         <p>
          <span class="flagicon">
           <img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="800" data-file-width="1200" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Flag_of_the_German_Empire.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_German_Empire.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Flag_of_the_German_Empire.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_German_Empire.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/ec/Flag_of_the_German_Empire.svg/45px-Flag_of_the_German_Empire.svg.png 2x" width="23"/>
          </span>
          <a href="/wiki/German_Empire" title="German Empire">
           German Empire
          </a>
          1899–1918
          <br/>
          <span class="flagicon">
           <img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="700" data-file-width="1000" height="15" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg/22px-Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg/33px-Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/3/30/Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg/43px-Flag_of_Japan_%281870-1999%29.svg.png 2x" width="22"/>
          </span>
          <a href="/wiki/Empire_of_Japan" title="Empire of Japan">
           Empire of Japan
          </a>
          1919–1947
          <br/>
          <span class="flagicon">
           <img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="900" data-file-width="1710" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281848-1851%29.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281848-1851%29.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281848-1851%29.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281848-1851%29.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/a/a4/Flag_of_the_United_States_%281848-1851%29.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_United_States_%281848-1851%29.svg.png 2x" width="23"/>
          </span>
          <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">
           United States
          </a>
          1947–1994
          <br/>
         </p>
         <span class="flagicon">
          <img alt="" class="thumbborder" data-file-height="400" data-file-width="760" height="12" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Flag_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia.svg/23px-Flag_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia.svg.png" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Flag_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia.svg/35px-Flag_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia.svg.png 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/e/e4/Flag_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia.svg/46px-Flag_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia.svg.png 2x" width="23"/>
         </span>
         <a class="mw-selflink selflink">
          Micronesia
         </a>
         1994–present
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The ancestors of the Micronesians settled over four thousand years ago. A decentralized chieftain-based system eventually evolved into a more centralized economic and religious culture centered on
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Yap_Island" title="Yap Island">
        Yap
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/Nan_Madol" title="Nan Madol">
        Nan Madol
       </a>
       , consisting of a series of small
       <a href="/wiki/Artificial_island" title="Artificial island">
        artificial islands
       </a>
       linked by a network of canals, is often called the Venice of the Pacific. It is located on the eastern periphery of the island of Pohnpei and used to be the ceremonial and political seat of the Saudeleur dynasty that united Pohnpei's estimated 25,000 people from about
       <a href="/wiki/Anno_Domini" title="Anno Domini">
        AD
       </a>
       500 until 1500, when the centralized system collapsed.
      </p>
      <p>
       European explorers—first the
       <a href="/wiki/Portugal" title="Portugal">
        Portuguese
       </a>
       in search of the
       <a href="/wiki/Maluku_Islands" title="Maluku Islands">
        Spice Islands
       </a>
       (
       <a href="/wiki/Indonesia" title="Indonesia">
        Indonesia
       </a>
       ) and then the
       <a href="/wiki/Spanish_Empire" title="Spanish Empire">
        Spanish
       </a>
       —reached the
       <a href="/wiki/Caroline_Islands" title="Caroline Islands">
        Carolines
       </a>
       in the sixteenth century. The Spanish incorporated the archipelago to the
       <a href="/wiki/Spanish_East_Indies" title="Spanish East Indies">
        Spanish East Indies
       </a>
       and in the 19th century established a number of outposts and missions. In 1887, they founded the town of
       <i>
        Santiago de la Ascension
       </i>
       in what today is
       <a href="/wiki/Kolonia" title="Kolonia">
        Kolonia
       </a>
       on the island of Pohnpei.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-5">
        <a href="#cite_note-5">
         [5]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Following defeat in the
       <a href="/wiki/Spanish%E2%80%93American_War" title="Spanish–American War">
        Spanish–American War
       </a>
       , the Spanish sold the archipelago to
       <a href="/wiki/German_Empire" title="German Empire">
        Germany
       </a>
       in 1899 under the
       <a href="/wiki/German%E2%80%93Spanish_Treaty_(1899)" title="German–Spanish Treaty (1899)">
        German–Spanish Treaty of 1899
       </a>
       . Germany incorporated it into
       <a href="/wiki/German_New_Guinea" title="German New Guinea">
        German New Guinea
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       During
       <a href="/wiki/World_War_I" title="World War I">
        World War I
       </a>
       , it was captured by
       <a href="/wiki/Empire_of_Japan" title="Empire of Japan">
        Japan
       </a>
       . Following the war, the
       <a href="/wiki/League_of_Nations" title="League of Nations">
        League of Nations
       </a>
       awarded a
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/League_of_Nations_Mandate" title="League of Nations Mandate">
        mandate
       </a>
       for Japan to administer the islands as part of the
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Nanyo_(Japanese_mandated_territory)" title="Nanyo (Japanese mandated territory)">
        South Pacific Mandate
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       During
       <a href="/wiki/World_War_II" title="World War II">
        World War II
       </a>
       , a significant portion of the Japanese fleet was based in
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Truk_Lagoon" title="Truk Lagoon">
        Truk Lagoon
       </a>
       . In February 1944,
       <a href="/wiki/Operation_Hailstone" title="Operation Hailstone">
        Operation Hailstone
       </a>
       , one of the most important naval battles of the war, took place at Truk, in which many Japanese support vessels and aircraft were destroyed.
      </p>
      <p>
       Following World War II, it was administered by the
       <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">
        United States
       </a>
       under
       <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">
        United Nations
       </a>
       auspices in 1947 as part of the
       <a href="/wiki/Trust_Territory_of_the_Pacific_Islands" title="Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands">
        Trust Territory of the Pacific Islands
       </a>
       pursuant to
       <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_21" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 21">
        Security Council Resolution 21
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <p>
       On May 10, 1979, four of the Trust Territory districts ratified a new constitution to become the Federated States of Micronesia.
       <a href="/wiki/Palau" title="Palau">
        Palau
       </a>
       , the
       <a href="/wiki/Marshall_Islands" title="Marshall Islands">
        Marshall Islands
       </a>
       , and the
       <a href="/wiki/Northern_Mariana_Islands" title="Northern Mariana Islands">
        Northern Mariana Islands
       </a>
       chose not to participate. The FSM signed a
       <a href="/wiki/Compact_of_Free_Association" title="Compact of Free Association">
        Compact of Free Association
       </a>
       with the United States, which entered into force on November 3, 1986, marking Micronesia's emergence from trusteeship to independence. Independence was formally concluded under international law in 1990, when the United Nations officially ended the Trusteeship status pursuant to
       <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council_Resolution_683" title="United Nations Security Council Resolution 683">
        Security Council Resolution 683
       </a>
       . The Compact was renewed in 2004.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Politics">
        Politics
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Federated_States_of_Micronesia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=2" title="Edit section: Politics">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Politics_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Politics of the Federated States of Micronesia">
        Politics of the Federated States of Micronesia
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       The Federated States of Micronesia is governed by the 1979 constitution, which guarantees fundamental human rights and establishes a separation of governmental powers. The unicameral Congress has fourteen members elected by popular vote. Four senators—one from each state—serve four-year terms; the remaining ten senators represent single-member districts based on population, and serve two-year terms. The President and Vice President are elected by Congress from among the four state-based senators to serve four-year terms in the executive branch. Their congressional seats are then filled by special elections.
      </p>
      <p>
       The president and vice president are supported by an appointed cabinet. There are no formal political parties.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Defense_and_foreign_affairs">
        Defense and foreign affairs
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Federated_States_of_Micronesia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=3" title="Edit section: Defense and foreign affairs">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Compact_of_Free_Association" title="Compact of Free Association">
        Compact of Free Association
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       In international politics, the Federated States of Micronesia has often voted with the United States with respect to
       <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly" title="United Nations General Assembly">
        United Nations General Assembly
       </a>
       resolutions.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-6">
        <a href="#cite_note-6">
         [6]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The FSM is a sovereign, self-governing state in
       <a href="/wiki/Associated_state" title="Associated state">
        free association
       </a>
       with the
       <a href="/wiki/United_States" title="United States">
        United States of America
       </a>
       , which is wholly responsible for its defense. The Division of Maritime Surveillance operates a paramilitary Maritime Wing and a small
       <a href="/wiki/Water_police" title="Water police">
        Maritime Police
       </a>
       Unit. The Compact of Free Association allows
       <a href="/wiki/Nationality_law_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Nationality law of the Federated States of Micronesia">
        FSM citizens
       </a>
       to join the U.S. military without having to obtain U.S. permanent residency or citizenship,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-7">
        <a href="#cite_note-7">
         [7]
        </a>
       </sup>
       allows for immigration and employment for Micronesians in the U.S., and establishes economic and technical aid programs.
      </p>
      <p>
       FSM has foreign relations with 56 countries, including the
       <a href="/wiki/Holy_See" title="Holy See">
        Holy See
       </a>
       . FSM was admitted to the
       <a href="/wiki/United_Nations" title="United Nations">
        United Nations
       </a>
       based on the
       <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_Security_Council" title="United Nations Security Council">
        Security Council
       </a>
       's recommendation on August 9, 1991 in Resolution 703 and the
       <a href="/wiki/United_Nations_General_Assembly" title="United Nations General Assembly">
        General Assembly
       </a>
       's approval on September 17, 1991 in Resolution 46/2.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-8">
        <a href="#cite_note-8">
         [8]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The FSM is an active member of the
       <a href="/wiki/Pacific_Islands_Forum" title="Pacific Islands Forum">
        Pacific Islands Forum
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-9">
        <a href="#cite_note-9">
         [9]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Administrative_divisions">
        Administrative divisions

       <span class="mw-editsection">

        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="thumb tright">

        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">

          </a>
         </div>
         A map of the Federated States of Micronesia.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:

        Administrative divisions of the Federated States of Micronesia
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       The four states in the federation are:
      </p>

      </table>
      <p>
       These states are further divided into
       <a href="/wiki/Municipality" title="Municipality">
        municipalities
       </a>
       .
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Geography">
        Geography
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Federated_States_of_Micronesia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" title="Edit section: Geography">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:302px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Koloniasokehs.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="953" data-file-width="1441" height="198" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Koloniasokehs.jpg/300px-Koloniasokehs.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Koloniasokehs.jpg/450px-Koloniasokehs.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/4/4d/Koloniasokehs.jpg/600px-Koloniasokehs.jpg 2x" width="300"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Koloniasokehs.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         A view of Kolonia Town from Sokehs Ridge in
         <a href="/wiki/Pohnpei" title="Pohnpei">
          Pohnpei
         </a>
         .
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Geography_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Geography of the Federated States of Micronesia">
        Geography of the Federated States of Micronesia
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       The Federated States of Micronesia consists of 607
       <a href="/wiki/Island" title="Island">
        islands
       </a>
       extending 2,900 km (1,802 mi) across the
       <a href="/wiki/Archipelago" title="Archipelago">
        archipelago
       </a>
       of the
       <a href="/wiki/Caroline_Islands" title="Caroline Islands">
        Caroline Islands
       </a>
       east of the
       <a href="/wiki/Philippines" title="Philippines">
        Philippines
       </a>
       . The islands have a combined area of 702 km
       <sup>
        2
       </sup>
       (271 sq mi).
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cia-fsm_13-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-cia-fsm-13">
         [13]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       The islands are grouped into four states, which are
       <a href="/wiki/Yap_State" title="Yap State">
        Yap
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Chuuk_State" title="Chuuk State">
        Chuuk
       </a>
       (called Truk until January 1990),
       <a href="/wiki/Pohnpei_State" title="Pohnpei State">
        Pohnpei
       </a>
       (known as "Ponape" until November 1984), and
       <a href="/wiki/Kosrae" title="Kosrae">
        Kosrae
       </a>
       (formerly Kusaie). These four states are each represented by a white star on the national flag. The capital is
       <a href="/wiki/Palikir" title="Palikir">
        Palikir
       </a>
       , on Pohnpei.
      </p>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Economy">
        Economy
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Federated_States_of_Micronesia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=6" title="Edit section: Economy">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Economy_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Economy of the Federated States of Micronesia">
        Economy of the Federated States of Micronesia
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       Economic activity in the Federated States of Micronesia consists primarily of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Subsistence_farming" title="Subsistence farming">
        subsistence farming
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Fishing" title="Fishing">
        fishing
       </a>
       . The islands have few mineral deposits worth exploiting, except for high-grade
       <a href="/wiki/Phosphate" title="Phosphate">
        phosphate
       </a>
       .
       <a href="/wiki/Longline_fishing" title="Longline fishing">
        Long line
       </a>
       fishing of
       <a href="/wiki/Tuna" title="Tuna">
        tuna
       </a>
       is also viable with foreign vessels from
       <a href="/wiki/China" title="China">
        China
       </a>
       operated in the 1990s. The potential for a
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Tourist_industry" title="Tourist industry">
        tourist industry
       </a>
       exists, but the remoteness of the location and a lack of adequate facilities hinder development.
       <a href="/wiki/United_States_foreign_aid" title="United States foreign aid">
        Financial assistance from the U.S.
       </a>
       is the primary source of revenue, with the U.S. pledged to spend $1.3 billion in the islands in 1986–2001;
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Manual_of_Style/Dates_and_numbers#Chronological_items" title="Wikipedia:Manual of Style/Dates and numbers">
          <span title="The date of the event predicted near this tag has passed. (June 2016)">
           needs update
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
       the
       <a href="/wiki/The_World_Factbook" title="The World Factbook">
        CIA World Factbook
       </a>
       lists high dependence on U.S. aid as one of the main concerns of the FSM.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-cia-fsm_13-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-cia-fsm-13">
         [13]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Geographical isolation and a poorly developed infrastructure are major impediments to long-term growth.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-14">
        <a href="#cite_note-14">
         [14]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Transportation">
        Transportation
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Federated_States_of_Micronesia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=7" title="Edit section: Transportation">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       The Federated States of Micronesia is served by four international airports.
      </p>
      <ul>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Pohnpei_International_Airport" title="Pohnpei International Airport">
         Pohnpei International Airport
        </a>
        , on the main island of
        <a href="/wiki/Pohnpei_State" title="Pohnpei State">
         Pohnpei State
        </a>
        .
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Chuuk_International_Airport" title="Chuuk International Airport">
         Chuuk International Airport
        </a>
        , located on the main island of
        <a href="/wiki/Chuuk_State" title="Chuuk State">
         Chuuk State
        </a>
        .
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Kosrae_International_Airport" title="Kosrae International Airport">
         Kosrae International Airport
        </a>
        , located on the main island of
        <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Kosrae_State" title="Kosrae State">
         Kosrae State
        </a>
        .
       </li>
       <li>
        <a href="/wiki/Yap_International_Airport" title="Yap International Airport">
         Yap International Airport
        </a>
        , located on the main island of
        <a href="/wiki/Yap_State" title="Yap State">
         Yap State
        </a>
        .
       </li>
      </ul>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Society">
        Society
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Federated_States_of_Micronesia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=8" title="Edit section: Society">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Demographics">
        Demographics
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Federated_States_of_Micronesia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=9" title="Edit section: Demographics">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Demographics_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Demographics of the Federated States of Micronesia">
        Demographics of the Federated States of Micronesia
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:242px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Ulithi-Dancers.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="750" data-file-width="1000" height="180" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Ulithi-Dancers.jpg/240px-Ulithi-Dancers.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Ulithi-Dancers.jpg/360px-Ulithi-Dancers.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/8/88/Ulithi-Dancers.jpg/480px-Ulithi-Dancers.jpg 2x" width="240"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Ulithi-Dancers.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         People performing a welcome ceremony on
         <a href="/wiki/Ulithi" title="Ulithi">
          Ulithi
         </a>
         atoll.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       The indigenous population of the nation, which is predominantly Micronesian, consists of various ethnolinguistic groups. It has a nearly 100% Pacific Islander and
       <a href="/wiki/Asian_people" title="Asian people">
        Asian
       </a>
       population:
       <a href="/wiki/Chuukese_people" title="Chuukese people">
        Chuukese
       </a>
       48.8%,
       <a href="/wiki/Pohnpeian_language" title="Pohnpeian language">
        Pohnpeian
       </a>
       24.2%,
       <a href="/wiki/Kosraean_language" title="Kosraean language">
        Kosraean
       </a>
       6.2%,
       <a href="/wiki/Yapese_people" title="Yapese people">
        Yapese
       </a>
       5.2%,
       <a href="/wiki/Yap" title="Yap">
        Yap
       </a>
       outer islands 4.5%,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Asian_ethnic_groups" title="Asian ethnic groups">
        Asian
       </a>
       1.8%,
       <a href="/wiki/Polynesians" title="Polynesians">
        Polynesian
       </a>
       1.5%, other 6.4%, unknown 1.4%. A sizeable minority also have some
       <a href="/wiki/Japanese_settlement_in_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Japanese settlement in the Federated States of Micronesia">
        Japanese ancestry
       </a>
       , which is a result of intermarriages between Japanese settlers and Micronesians during the Japanese colonial period.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-15">
        <a href="#cite_note-15">
         [15]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       There is also a growing expatriate population of Americans, Australians, Europeans, and residents from China and the Philippines since the 1990s.
       <a href="/wiki/English_language" title="English language">
        English
       </a>
       has become the common language of the government, and for secondary and tertiary education. Outside of the main capital towns of the four FSM states, the local languages are primarily spoken. Population growth remains high at more than 3% annually, offset somewhat by net emigration.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Languages">
        Languages
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Federated_States_of_Micronesia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=10" title="Edit section: Languages">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       English is the official and common language. Also spoken are
       <a href="/wiki/Chuukese_language" title="Chuukese language">
        Chuukese
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Kosraean_language" title="Kosraean language">
        Kosraean
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Pohnpeian_language" title="Pohnpeian language">
        Pohnpeian
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Yapese_language" title="Yapese language">
        Yapese
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Ulithian_language" title="Ulithian language">
        Ulithian
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Woleaian_language" title="Woleaian language">
        Woleaian
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Nukuoro_language" title="Nukuoro language">
        Nukuoro
       </a>
       , and
       <a href="/wiki/Kapingamarangi_language" title="Kapingamarangi language">
        Kapingamarangi
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-16">
        <a href="#cite_note-16">
         [16]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Other languages spoken in the country include
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Pingelapese" title="Pingelapese">
        Pingelapese
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Ngatikese" title="Ngatikese">
        Ngatikese
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Satawalese_language" title="Satawalese language">
        Satawalese
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Puluwatese_language" title="Puluwatese language">
        Puluwatese
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Mortlockese_language" title="Mortlockese language">
        Mortlockese
       </a>
       , and
       <a href="/wiki/Mokilese_language" title="Mokilese language">
        Mokilese
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2013)">
           citation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
       There are about 3,000 speakers of
       <a href="/wiki/Kapingamarangi_language" title="Kapingamarangi language">
        Kapingamarangi
       </a>
       and
       <a href="/wiki/Ulithian_language" title="Ulithian language">
        Ulithian
       </a>
       , and under 1,000 speakers of
       <a href="/wiki/Nukuoro_language" title="Nukuoro language">
        Nukuoro
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="noprint Inline-Template Template-Fact" style="white-space:nowrap;">
        [
        <i>
         <a href="/wiki/Wikipedia:Citation_needed" title="Wikipedia:Citation needed">
          <span title="This claim needs references to reliable sources. (September 2013)">
           citation needed
          </span>
         </a>
        </i>
        ]
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Religion">
        Religion
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Federated_States_of_Micronesia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" title="Edit section: Religion">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       Main article:
       <a href="/wiki/Religion_in_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Religion in the Federated States of Micronesia">
        Religion in the Federated States of Micronesia
       </a>
      </div>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:242px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Operation_Christmas_Drop_2008_081219-F-6911G-440.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="1949" data-file-width="2700" height="173" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Operation_Christmas_Drop_2008_081219-F-6911G-440.jpg/240px-Operation_Christmas_Drop_2008_081219-F-6911G-440.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Operation_Christmas_Drop_2008_081219-F-6911G-440.jpg/360px-Operation_Christmas_Drop_2008_081219-F-6911G-440.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/0/0b/Operation_Christmas_Drop_2008_081219-F-6911G-440.jpg/480px-Operation_Christmas_Drop_2008_081219-F-6911G-440.jpg 2x" width="240"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Operation_Christmas_Drop_2008_081219-F-6911G-440.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         The US airforce has
         <a href="/wiki/Operation_Christmas_Drop" title="Operation Christmas Drop">
          dropped presents and humanitarian aid to the islands
         </a>
         every Christmas since 1952.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <p>
       Most Micronesians are
       <a href="/wiki/Christian" title="Christian">
        Christian
       </a>
       . Several
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Protestant" title="Protestant">
        Protestant
       </a>
       denominations, as well as the
       <a href="/wiki/Roman_Catholic_(term)" title="Roman Catholic (term)">
        Roman
       </a>
       <a href="/wiki/Catholic_Church" title="Catholic Church">
        Catholic Church
       </a>
       , are present in every Micronesian state.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_17-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-report-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Most Protestant groups trace their roots to American Congregationalist missionaries.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_17-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-report-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
       On the island of Kosrae, the population is approximately 7,800; 95 percent are Protestants.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_17-2">
        <a href="#cite_note-report-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
       On
       <a href="/wiki/Pohnpei" title="Pohnpei">
        Pohnpei
       </a>
       , the population of 35,000 is evenly divided between Protestants and Catholics.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_17-3">
        <a href="#cite_note-report-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       On Chuuk and Yap, an estimated 60 percent are Catholic and 40 percent are Protestant.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_17-4">
        <a href="#cite_note-report-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Religious groups with small followings include
       <a href="/wiki/Baptists" title="Baptists">
        Baptists
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Assemblies_of_God" title="Assemblies of God">
        Assemblies of God
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Salvation_Army" title="Salvation Army">
        Salvation Army
       </a>
       ,
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Seventh-day_Adventists" title="Seventh-day Adventists">
        Seventh-day Adventists
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/Jehovah%27s_Witnesses" title="Jehovah's Witnesses">
        Jehovah's Witnesses
       </a>
       ,
       <a href="/wiki/The_Church_of_Jesus_Christ_of_Latter-day_Saints" title="The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints">
        The Church of Jesus Christ of Latter-day Saints
       </a>
       (Mormons), and the
       <a href="/wiki/Bah%C3%A1%27%C3%AD_Faith" title="Bahá'í Faith">
        Bahá'í Faith
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_17-5">
        <a href="#cite_note-report-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
       There is a small group of
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Buddhists" title="Buddhists">
        Buddhists
       </a>
       on Pohnpei,
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_17-6">
        <a href="#cite_note-report-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
       and a small group of
       <a href="/wiki/Ahmadiyya" title="Ahmadiyya">
        Ahmadiyya Muslims
       </a>
       in Kosrae.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-18">
        <a href="#cite_note-18">
         [18]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Attendance at religious services is generally high;
       <a href="/wiki/Church_(building)" title="Church (building)">
        churches
       </a>
       are well supported by their congregations and play a significant role in civil society.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_17-7">
        <a href="#cite_note-report-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <p>
       Most immigrants are Filipino Catholics who have joined local Catholic churches.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_17-8">
        <a href="#cite_note-report-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The Filipino
       <a href="/wiki/Iglesia_ni_Cristo" title="Iglesia ni Cristo">
        Iglesia ni Cristo
       </a>
       also has a church in Pohnpei.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_17-9">
        <a href="#cite_note-report-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
       In the 1890s, on the island of Pohnpei, intermissionary conflicts and the conversion of clan leaders resulted in religious divisions along clan lines which persist today.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_17-10">
        <a href="#cite_note-report-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
       More Protestants live on the western side of the island, while more Catholics live on the eastern side.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_17-11">
        <a href="#cite_note-report-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <a class="mw-redirect" href="/wiki/Missionaries" title="Missionaries">
        Missionaries
       </a>
       of many religious traditions are present and operate freely.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_17-12">
        <a href="#cite_note-report-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The Constitution provides for
       <a href="/wiki/Freedom_of_religion" title="Freedom of religion">
        freedom of religion
       </a>
       , and the Government generally respected this right in practice.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_17-13">
        <a href="#cite_note-report-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
       The US government received no reports of societal abuses or discrimination based on religious belief or practice in 2007.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-report_17-14">
        <a href="#cite_note-report-17">
         [17]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Health">
        Health
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Federated_States_of_Micronesia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=12" title="Edit section: Health">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       <a href="/wiki/Pingelap" title="Pingelap">
        Pingelap
       </a>
       in Pohnpei State is notable for the prevalence of an extreme form of
       <a href="/wiki/Color_blindness" title="Color blindness">
        color blindness
       </a>
       called
       <a href="/wiki/Achromatopsia" title="Achromatopsia">
        Achromatopsia
       </a>
       , and known locally as
       <a href="/wiki/Pingelap#Color-blindness" title="Pingelap">
        maskun
       </a>
       .
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Brody_1970_19-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Brody_1970-19">
         [19]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hussels_1972_20-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-Hussels_1972-20">
         [20]
        </a>
       </sup>
       Approximately 5% of the atoll's 3000 inhabitants are afflicted.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Brody_1970_19-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-Brody_1970-19">
         [19]
        </a>
       </sup>
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-Hussels_1972_20-1">
        <a href="#cite_note-Hussels_1972-20">
         [20]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <div class="thumb tright">
       <div class="thumbinner" style="width:242px;">
        <a class="image" href="/wiki/File:Yap_Stone_Money.jpg">
         <img alt="" class="thumbimage" data-file-height="732" data-file-width="900" height="195" src="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/Yap_Stone_Money.jpg/240px-Yap_Stone_Money.jpg" srcset="//upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/Yap_Stone_Money.jpg/360px-Yap_Stone_Money.jpg 1.5x, //upload.wikimedia.org/wikipedia/commons/thumb/5/54/Yap_Stone_Money.jpg/480px-Yap_Stone_Money.jpg 2x" width="240"/>
        </a>
        <div class="thumbcaption">
         <div class="magnify">
          <a class="internal" href="/wiki/File:Yap_Stone_Money.jpg" title="Enlarge">
          </a>
         </div>
         A large (approximately 2.4 m or about 8 ft in height) example of Yapese stone money (
         <a href="/wiki/Rai_stones" title="Rai stones">
          Rai stones
         </a>
         ) in the village of Gachpar.
        </div>
       </div>
      </div>
      <h2>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Culture">
        Culture
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Federated_States_of_Micronesia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=13" title="Edit section: Culture">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h2>
      <div class="hatnote navigation-not-searchable" role="note">
       See also:
       <a href="/wiki/Music_of_the_Federated_States_of_Micronesia" title="Music of the Federated States of Micronesia">
        Music of the Federated States of Micronesia
       </a>
      </div>
      <p>
       Each of the four states has its own culture and traditions, but there are also common cultural and economic bonds that are centuries old. Cultural similarities include the importance of the traditional extended family and clan systems and are found on all the islands.
      </p>
      <p>
       The island of Yap is notable for its "stone money" (
       <a href="/wiki/Rai_stones" title="Rai stones">
        Rai stones
       </a>
       ), large disks usually of calcite, up to 4 meters (13 ft) in diameter, with a hole in the middle. The islanders, aware of the owner of a piece, do not necessarily move them when ownership changes. There are five major types:
       <i>
        Mmbul
       </i>
       ,
       <i>
        Gaw
       </i>
       ,
       <i>
        Ray
       </i>
       ,
       <i>
        Yar
       </i>
       , and
       <i>
        Reng
       </i>
       , the last being only 30 cm (12 in) in diameter. Their value is based on both size and history, many of them having been brought from other islands, as far as
       <a href="/wiki/New_Guinea" title="New Guinea">
        New Guinea
       </a>
       , but most coming in ancient times from
       <a href="/wiki/Palau" title="Palau">
        Palau
       </a>
       . Approximately 6,500 of them are scattered around the island.
      </p>
      <h3>
       <span class="mw-headline" id="Literature">
        Literature
       </span>
       <span class="mw-editsection">
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         [
        </span>
        <a href="/w/index.php?title=Federated_States_of_Micronesia&amp;action=edit&amp;section=14" title="Edit section: Literature">
         edit
        </a>
        <span class="mw-editsection-bracket">
         ]
        </span>
       </span>
      </h3>
      <p>
       There have been few published literary writers from the Federated States of Micronesia.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-21">
        <a href="#cite_note-21">
         [21]
        </a>
       </sup>
       In 2008,
       <a href="/wiki/Emelihter_Kihleng" title="Emelihter Kihleng">
        Emelihter Kihleng
       </a>
       became the first ever Micronesian to publish a collection of poetry in the English language.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-22">
        <a href="#cite_note-22">
         [22]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
      <h2>

                     </span>
